For two lines to be perpendicular, the product of their slopes must be $-1$, so the perpendicular line must have a slope of $-2$. The equation $x - my + 1 = 0$ can be rewritten as $y = \\frac{1}{m}x + \\frac{1}{m}$. Equating the slope gives $\\frac{1}{m} = -2$, which implies $m = -\\frac{1}{2}$. ",
